}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

  decreases |s|

  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  // The proof is trivial by definition of Flatten
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  // The proof is trivial by definition of Flatten
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0

  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2

  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{

    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b

  assert Flatten([a]) == a;

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
  assert Flatten([x]) == [x][..0] + [x][0];
  assert Flatten([x]) == [] + x;
  assert Flatten([x]) == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{

  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  assert Flatten([a, b]) == Flatten([a]) + [a, b][1];

  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  // Flatten([x]) = Flatten([]) + x = "" + x = x
  assert Flatten([]) == "";
  assert Flatten([x]) == "" + x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  // Flatten([a, b]) = Flatten([a]) + b = a + b
  assert Flatten([a]) == a;
  assert Flatten([a, b]) == a + b;
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
    assert AllGood(parts);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
    assert AllGood(parts);
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    // Flatten proof
    assert Flatten([s]) == s;
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    assert Flatten([first, second]) == first + second;

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert CountChar(first, '0') != CountChar(first, '1');

    // second is good: single character
    assert CountChar(second, '0') != CountChar(second, '1');
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

{

}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountChar(s: string, c: char): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else CountChar(s[..|s|-1], c) + (if s[|s|-1] == c then 1 else 0)
}

ghost predicate IsGood(s: string)
{
  CountChar(s, '0') != CountChar(s, '1')
}

ghost predicate IsBinaryString(s: string)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == '0' || s[i] == '1'
}

ghost function Flatten(parts: seq<string>): string
  decreases |parts|
{
  if |parts| == 0 then ""
  else Flatten(parts[..|parts|-1]) + parts[|parts|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllGood(parts: seq<string>)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |parts| :: IsGood(parts[i])
}

lemma CountCharSum(s: string)
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures CountChar(s, '0') + CountChar(s, '1') == |s|
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountCharSum(s[..|s|-1]);
  }
}

lemma FlattenSingleton(x: string)
  ensures Flatten([x]) == x
{
  assert [x][..0] == [];
  assert [x][0] == x;
}

lemma FlattenPair(a: string, b: string)
  ensures Flatten([a, b]) == a + b
{
  assert [a, b][..1] == [a];
  assert [a, b][1] == b;
  FlattenSingleton(a);
}

method KeanuReeves(s: string) returns (k: int, parts: seq<string>)
  requires |s| > 0
  requires IsBinaryString(s)
  ensures k == |parts|
  ensures k == 1 || k == 2
  ensures Flatten(parts) == s
  ensures AllGood(parts)
  ensures k == 1 <==> IsGood(s)
{
  var zeros := 0;
  var ones := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant zeros == CountChar(s[..i], '0')
    invariant ones == CountChar(s[..i], '1')
  {
    if s[i] == '0' {
      zeros := zeros + 1;
    } else {
      ones := ones + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  if zeros != ones {
    k := 1;
    parts := [s];
    FlattenSingleton(s);
  } else {
    k := 2;
    var first := s[..|s| - 1];
    var second := [s[|s| - 1]];
    parts := [first, second];

    // Flatten proof
    assert first + second == s;
    FlattenPair(first, second);

    // first is good: odd-length binary string can't have equal counts
    CountCharSum(s);
    CountCharSum(first);
    assert IsGood(first);

    // second is good: single character
    assert IsGood(second);
  }
}
